\hypertarget{structed__state__vars_1_1patchtype}{}\doxysection{ed\+\_\+state\+\_\+vars\+::patchtype Type Reference}
\label{structed__state__vars_1_1patchtype}\index{ed\_state\_vars::patchtype@{ed\_state\_vars::patchtype}}


Contains arrays of cohorts that populate the current patch. ~\newline
 This is the lowest (most nested) part of the memory structure. ~\newline

\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
Contains arrays of cohorts that populate the current patch. ~\newline
 This is the lowest (most nested) part of the memory structure. ~\newline
 

Diagnostic variables averaged over various time scales bear the naming pattern as follows\+: ~\newline
 FMEAN -- averaged over FRQSUM (the least between FRQFAST, FRQSTATE and one day).~\newline
 DMEAN -- daily averages~\newline
 MMEAN -- monthly averages~\newline
 MMSQU -- monthly mean sum of squares~\newline
 QMEAN -- mean diel~\newline
 QMSQU -- mean diel (mean sum of squares)~\newline
~\newline
 pl means plant (intensive variable)~\newline
 m2l means m2 of leaf area (intensive variable)~\newline
 m2g means m2 of ground area (extensive variable)~\newline

Relative carbon balance\+:~\newline
. 

\[ \frac{1}{cbr\_bar} = k * \frac{cb\_lightmax}{cb} + (1 - k) * \frac{cb\_moistmax}{cb} \]~\newline
k is the ddmort\+\_\+const given on the namelist \mbox{\Hypertarget{structed__state__vars_1_1patchtype_a1964bd21422283e16bc404ac95ff7cb7}\label{structed__state__vars_1_1patchtype_a1964bd21422283e16bc404ac95ff7cb7}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{census\_status}{census\_status}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily integer, dimension(\+:), pointer ed\+\_\+state\+\_\+vars\+::patchtype\+::census\+\_\+status}



census\+\_\+status codes (updated every census)\+: ~\newline
0 -\/ this cohort has never been with DBH \texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} 10 cm at census times ~\newline
1 -\/ New recruit (DBH \texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} 10 cm for the first census) ~\newline
2 -\/ Established (DBH \texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} 10 cm for at least two censuses ~\newline
